	:KUBE-SERVICES - [0:0]
	:KUBE-POSTROUTING - [0:0]
	:KUBE-NODE-PORT - [0:0]
	:KUBE-LOAD-BALANCER - [0:0]
	:KUBE-MARK-MASQ - [0:0]
	-A KUBE-SERVICES -s ::1/128 -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-SERVICES -m addrtype --dst-type LOCAL -j KUBE-NODE-PORT
	-A KUBE-LOAD-BALANCER -j KUBE-MARK-MASQ
	-A KUBE-POSTROUTING -m mark ! --mark 0x00004000/0x00004000 -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-POSTROUTING -j MARK --xor-mark 0x00004000
	-A KUBE-POSTROUTING -m comment --comment "kubernetes service traffic requiring SNAT" -j MASQUERADE --random-fully
	-A KUBE-MARK-MASQ -j MARK --or-mark 0x00004000
	COMMIT
	*filter
	:KUBE-FORWARD - [0:0]
	:KUBE-NODE-PORT - [0:0]
	:KUBE-PROXY-FIREWALL - [0:0]
	:KUBE-SOURCE-RANGES-FIREWALL - [0:0]
	:KUBE-IPVS-FILTER - [0:0]
	-A KUBE-SOURCE-RANGES-FIREWALL -j DROP
	-A KUBE-FORWARD -m comment --comment "kubernetes forwarding rules" -m mark --mark 0x00004000/0x00004000 -j ACCEPT
	-A KUBE-FORWARD -m comment --comment "kubernetes forwarding conntrack rule" -m conntrack --ctstate RELATED,ESTABLISHED -j ACCEPT
	-A KUBE-NODE-PORT -m comment --comment "Kubernetes health check node port" -m set --match-set KUBE-6-HEALTH-CHECK-NODE-PORT dst -j ACCEPT
	-A KUBE-IPVS-FILTER -m set --match-set KUBE-6-LOAD-BALANCER dst,dst -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-IPVS-FILTER -m set --match-set KUBE-6-CLUSTER-IP dst,dst -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-IPVS-FILTER -m set --match-set KUBE-6-EXTERNAL-IP dst,dst -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-IPVS-FILTER -m set --match-set KUBE-6-HEALTH-CHECK-NODE-PORT dst -j RETURN
	-A KUBE-IPVS-FILTER -m conntrack --ctstate NEW -m set --match-set KUBE-6-IPVS-IPS dst -j REJECT
	COMMIT
